
## Vector Loads and Stores Functions:

### [Vector Unit-Stride Load Functions](../rvv-intrinsic-api.md#74-vector-unit-stride-operations):

**Prototypes:**

``` C
vfloat64m2_t vle64_v_f64m2_mu (vbool32_t mask, vfloat64m2_t maskedoff, const float64_t *base, size_t vl);
vfloat64m4_t vle64_v_f64m4_mu (vbool16_t mask, vfloat64m4_t maskedoff, const float64_t *base, size_t vl);

vuint64m2_t vle64_v_u64m2_mu (vbool32_t mask, vuint64m2_t maskedoff, const uint64_t *base, size_t vl);
vuint64m4_t vle64_v_u64m4_mu (vbool16_t mask, vuint64m4_t maskedoff, const uint64_t *base, size_t vl);
vuint64m8_t vle64_v_u64m8_mu (vbool8_t mask, vuint64m8_t maskedoff, const uint64_t *base, size_t vl);
```

### [Vector Unit-Stride Store Functions](../rvv-intrinsic-api.md#74-vector-unit-stride-operations):
This operation don't have Policy Intrinsic Functions.

### [Vector Strided Load Functions](../rvv-intrinsic-api.md#75-vector-strided-loadstore-operations):

### [Vector Strided Store Functions](../rvv-intrinsic-api.md#75-vector-strided-loadstore-operations):
This operation don't have Policy Intrinsic Functions.

### [Vector Indexed Load Functions](../rvv-intrinsic-api.md#76-vector-indexed-loadstore-operations):

**Prototypes:**
``` C
vfloat16mf4_t vloxei8_tu (vfloat16mf4_t maskedoff, const float16_t *base, vuint8mf8_t bindex, size_t vl);
vfloat16mf2_t vloxei8_tu (vfloat16mf2_t maskedoff, const float16_t *base, vuint8mf4_t bindex, size_t vl);
vfloat16m1_t vloxei8_tu (vfloat16m1_t maskedoff, const float16_t *base, vuint8mf2_t bindex, size_t vl);
vfloat16m2_t vloxei8_tu (vfloat16m2_t maskedoff, const float16_t *base, vuint8m1_t bindex, size_t vl);

vuint64m1_t vluxei32_mu (vbool64_t mask, vuint64m1_t maskedoff, const uint64_t *base, vuint32mf2_t bindex, size_t vl);

vuint64m8_t vluxei64_mu (vbool8_t mask, vuint64m8_t maskedoff, const uint64_t *base, vuint64m8_t bindex, size_t vl);
```

### [Vector Indexed Store Functions](../rvv-intrinsic-api.md#76-vector-indexed-loadstore-operations):
This operation don't have Policy Intrinsic Functions.

### [Unit-stride Fault-Only-First Loads Functions](../rvv-intrinsic-api.md#77-unit-stride-fault-only-first-loads-operations):

**Prototypes:**
